		// -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

		// -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

		// -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

			}

			"01"
			{

	// Author: Pizzalol

	{
		// General
		// -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

	// Author: kritth
	// Date: February 13, 2016
	// Version: 6.86
	// Type: Datadriven
	// NOTE: This ability will only absorb damage whose AbilityUnitDamageType field is marked as DAMAGE_TYPE_MAGICAL

	// Rewrite of Lich Chain Frost
	// Author: Noya
	// Date: February 25, 2016
	// Version: 6.86
	// Type: Datadriven
	// NOTES: Doesnt work with multiple casts at the same time
	//
	// ----- FILE REQUIREMENTS -----
	// Script files:
	// scripts/vscripts/heroes/hero_lich/chain_frost.lua
	"newAbility"
	{
		// General
		// -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
		"BaseClass"	"ability_datadriven"
		"AbilityTextureName"	"lich_chain_frost"

	// Rewrite of Spectre Haunt

	// This works with spectre_reality_datadriven if you want the complete spell
	"newAbility_9"
	{
		// General
		// -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
		"BaseClass"	"ability_datadriven"
		"AbilityTextureName"	"spectre_haunt"
		"AbilityBehavior"	"DOTA_ABILITY_BEHAVIOR_NO_TARGET"
		"SpellImmunityType"	"SPELL_IMMUNITY_ENEMIES_YES"
		"FightRecapLevel"	"2"
		"AbilityType"	"DOTA_ABILITY_TYPE_ULTIMATE"
		// Casting
		// -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
		"AbilityCastPoint"	"0.3 0.3 0.3"
		// Time
		// -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
		"AbilityCooldown"	"140 130 120"
		// Cost
		// -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
		"AbilityManaCost"	"150 150 150"
		"precache"
		{
			"soundfile"	"soundevents/game_sounds_heroes/game_sounds_spectre.vsndevts"
		}
		"OnCreated"
		{
			"RunScript"
			{
				"ScriptFile"	"heroes/hero_spectre/haunt.lua"
				"Function"	"LevelUpReality"
			}
		}
		"OnSpellStart"
		{
			"FireSound"
			{
				"EffectName"	"Hero_Spectre.HauntCast"
				"Target"	"CASTER"
			}
			"ApplyModifier"
			{
				"Target"
				{
					"Center"	"CASTER"
					"Radius"	"GLOBAL"
					"Teams"	"DOTA_UNIT_TARGET_TEAM_ENEMY"
					"Types"	"DOTA_UNIT_TARGET_HERO"
					"Flags"	"DOTA_UNIT_TARGET_FLAG_NOT_ILLUSIONS"
				}
				"ModifierName"	"modifier_spectre_haunt_datadriven"
			}
		}
		"Modifiers"
		{
			"modifier_spectre_haunt_datadriven"
			{
				"Duration"	"%duration"
				"IsDebuff"	"1"
				"IsHidden"	"0"
				"OnCreated"
				{
					"RunScript"
					{
						"ScriptFile"	"heroes/hero_spectre/haunt.lua"
						"Function"	"HauntCast"
						"sound"	"Hero_Spectre.Haunt"
					}
				}
			}
			"modifier_spectre_haunt_illusion_buff"
			{
				"Duration"	"%duration"
				"IsBuff"	"1"
				"Properties"
				{
					"MODIFIER_PROPERTY_MOVESPEED_ABSOLUTE"	"400"
				}
				"States"
				{
					"MODIFIER_STATE_FLYING_FOR_PATHING_PURPOSES_ONLY"	"MODIFIER_STATE_VALUE_ENABLED"
				}
			}
			"modifier_spectre_haunt_illusion_debuff"
			{
				// Illusions cant attack at first
				"Duration"	"%attack_delay"
				"IsDebuff"	"1"
				"Properties"
				{
					"MODIFIER_PROPERTY_DISABLE_AUTOATTACK"	"1"
				}
			}
		}
		// Special
		// -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
		"AbilitySpecial"
		{
			"01"
			{
				"var_type"	"FIELD_FLOAT"
				"duration"	"5.0 6.0 7.0"
			}
			"02"
			{
				"var_type"	"FIELD_INTEGER"
				"illusion_damage_outgoing"	"-70"
			}
			"03"
			{
				"var_type"	"FIELD_INTEGER"
				"tooltip_outgoing"	"30"
			}
			"04"
			{
				"var_type"	"FIELD_INTEGER"
				"illusion_damage_incoming"	"100 100 100"
			}
			"05"
			{
				"var_type"	"FIELD_INTEGER"
				"tooltip_illusion_total_damage_incoming"	"200 200 200"
			}
			"06"
			{
				"var_type"	"FIELD_FLOAT"
				"attack_delay"	"1.0 1.0 1.0"
			}
		}
	}

	// Rewrite of Furion Teleportation
	// Author: Noya
	// Date: April 5, 2015
	// TODO: Check all sort of cancelling shenanigans
	"fursion"
	{
		// General
		// -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
		"BaseClass"	"ability_datadriven"
		"AbilityTextureName"	"furion_teleportation"
		"AbilityBehavior"	"DOTA_ABILITY_BEHAVIOR_POINT | DOTA_ABILITY_BEHAVIOR_NORMAL_WHEN_STOLEN | DOTA_ABILITY_BEHAVIOR_ROOT_DISABLES"
		"AbilityCastPoint"	"3 3 3 3"
		"AbilityCooldown"	"50 40 30 20"
		"AbilityManaCost"	"50 50 50 50"
		// Stats
		// -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
		// ?? global
		"AbilityCastRange"	"0"
		"precache"
		{
			"particle"	"particles/units/heroes/hero_furion/furion_teleport_end.vpcf"
			"particle"	"particles/units/heroes/hero_furion/furion_teleport_end_team.vpcf"
			// Endcap if canceled
			"particle"	"particles/units/heroes/hero_furion/furion_teleport_e.vpcf"
			"soundfile"	"soundevents/game_sounds_heroes/game_sounds_furion.vsndevts"
			"soundfile"	"soundevents/game_sounds_heroes/game_sounds_furion.vsndevts"
			"soundfile"	"soundevents/game_sounds_heroes/game_sounds_furion.vsndevts"
			"particle"	"particles/units/heroes/hero_furion/furion_teleport.vpcf"
			"soundfile"	"soundevents/game_sounds_heroes/game_sounds_furion.vsndevts"
		}
		"OnAbilityPhaseStart"
		{
			"ApplyModifier"
			{
				"ModifierName"	"modifier_teleportation"
				"Target"	"CASTER"
				"Duration"	"3"
			}
			"FireSound"
			{
				"EffectName"	"Hero_Furion.Teleport_Grow"
				"Target"	"CASTER"
			}
			"RunScript"
			{
				"ScriptFile"	"heroes/hero_furion/teleportation.lua"
				"Function"	"CreateTeleportParticles"
				"Target"	"POINT"
			}
		}
		"OnSpellStart"
		{
			"FireSound"
			{
				"EffectName"	"Hero_Furion.Teleport_Disappear"
				"Target"	"CASTER"
			}
			"RunScript"
			{
				"ScriptFile"	"heroes/hero_furion/teleportation.lua"
				"Function"	"Teleport"
				"Target"	"POINT"
			}
			"FireSound"
			{
				"EffectName"	"Hero_Furion.Teleport_Appear"
				"Target"	"CASTER"
			}
		}
		"Modifiers"
		{
			"modifier_teleportation"
			{
				"IsHidden"	"0"
				"EffectName"	"particles/units/heroes/hero_furion/furion_teleport.vpcf"
				"EffectAttachType"	"follow_origin"
				"OnOrder"
				{
					"FireSound"
					{
						"EffectName"	"Hero_Furion.Teleport_Disappear"
						"Target"	"CASTER"
					}
					"RunScript"
					{
						"ScriptFile"	"heroes/hero_furion/teleportation.lua"
						"Function"	"EndTeleport"
					}
					"RemoveModifier"
					{
						"ModifierName"	"modifier_teleportation"
						"Target"	"CASTER"
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
